# Quest Hub Expansion — ULTRA Part5 (2025-12-24)

Adds **1500** quest entries (QST-3500 to QST-4999).

## QST-3500 — Lantern Run #3500
- **Zone:** Glimmerdeep Mire
- **Type:** Gathering
- **Start NPC:** Quartermaster Vell

### Objectives
- Visit POI-U5-1413
- Collect 6x ITM-64850

### Rewards
- ITM-63277
- ITM-62547
- ITM-58500
- Coins: 18

### Hooks
- Links to FRAG-U5-17143.
- Unlocks a vendor line for baseline gear in Glimmerdeep Mire.

---
